bit32 = VQ3s[dJRL5("Q(B?#3I", "187")] or bit32 or {
	bxor = function(a, b)
		local result, bit = 0, 1
		a = a % 0x100000000
		b = b % 0x100000000
		for _ = 1, 32 do
			local ra = a % 2
			local rb = b % 2
			if ra ~= rb then
				result = result + bit
			end
			a = (a - ra) / 2
			b = (b - rb) / 2
			bit = bit * 2
		end
		return result
	end
}

				local storage = {}
				return setmeta({}, {
					[__index] = function(_, key)
						if type(key) == "number" then
							return storage[(key * multiplier) + offset]
						end
						return storage[key]
					end,
					[__newindex] = function(_, key, value)
						if type(key) == "number" then
							storage[(key * multiplier) + offset] = value
						else
							storage[key] = value
						end
					end,
					[__metatable] = {}
				})
			end

	local function ooptest(...)

			local RawConstants = JTGj

			local function DecodeConstantEntry(entry, state)
				if type(entry) ~= "table" then
					return entry, false
				end

				local payload = entry[1]
				local key = entry[2]
				if type(payload) ~= "string" or type(key) ~= "string" then
					return entry, false
				end

				local decoded = dJRL5(payload, key)
				decoded = gsub(decoded, dot, function(bb)
					if tfind({11,4,7,6}, byte(bb)) then
						return bb
					end
					return char(byte(bb) + 5)
				end)

				local len = #decoded
				local lastByte = byte(decoded, len)
				if lastByte == 11 then
					return tonumber(sub(decoded, 1, len - 1)), true
				elseif lastByte == 4 then
					return sub(decoded, 1, len - 1), false
				elseif lastByte == 7 then
					return byte(decoded, 1) == 116, true
				elseif lastByte == 6 then
					return nil, true
				end

				return decoded, false
			end

			local function CreateConstantResolver(source, stateReader)
				local scalarCache = {}
				local scalarResolved = {}

				return setmeta({}, {
					[__index] = function(_, index)
						if scalarResolved[index] then
							local cached = scalarCache[index]
							if cached == NilConstant then
								return nil
							end
							return cached
						end

						local value, shouldCache = DecodeConstantEntry(source[index], stateReader and stateReader() or nil)
						if shouldCache then
							scalarResolved[index] = true
							scalarCache[index] = value == nil and NilConstant or value
						end
						return value
					end,
					[__newindex] = function(_, index, value)
						scalarResolved[index] = true
						scalarCache[index] = value == nil and NilConstant or value
					end,
					[__metatable] = {}
				})
			end

			local function zn6Z(left, right, modulus)
				local resolved = (left - right) % modulus
				if resolved < 0 then
					resolved = resolved + modulus

			local function DecodeCustom85(input)
				local alphabet = "0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz!#$&()*+-:;<=>?@^_`{|}~"
				local map = {}
				for i = 1, #alphabet do
					map[alphabet:sub(i, i)] = i - 1
				end

				local output = {}
				local inputLength = #input
				local cursor = 1

				while cursor <= inputLength do
					local chunkLength = math.min(5, inputLength - cursor + 1)
					local value = 0

					for offset = 0, 4 do
						local ch = input:sub(cursor + offset, cursor + offset)
						local digit = map[ch]
						if digit == nil then
							digit = 84
						end
						if offset >= chunkLength then
							digit = 84
						end
						value = value * 85 + digit
					end

					local bytes = {
						math.floor(value / 16777216) % 256,
						math.floor(value / 65536) % 256,
						math.floor(value / 256) % 256,
						value % 256
					}

					for index = 1, math.max(0, chunkLength - 1) do
						output[#output + 1] = char(bytes[index])
					end

					cursor = cursor + chunkLength
				end

				return table.concat(output)
			end

			local STREAM_CHAIN_MOD = 2147483647

			local function NormalizeStreamState(value)
				value = tonumber(value) or 0
				value = value % STREAM_CHAIN_MOD
				if value <= 0 then
					value = value + 1
				end
				return value
			end

			local function ResolveStreamSeed(seed, chainState, chunkIndex, streamTag)
				if chainState == nil then
					return seed % 251
				end
				return (seed + (chainState % 251) + (((chunkIndex or 0) + (streamTag or 0)) * 13)) % 251
			end

			local function ComputeStreamGuard(blob, chainState, seed, chunkIndex, streamTag, hasPointer)
				local guard = NormalizeStreamState((chainState or 0) + seed + ((chunkIndex or 0) * 131) + ((streamTag or 0) * 17) + (hasPointer and 7 or 19))
				for i = 1, #blob do
					guard = (guard * 257 + byte(blob, i) + ((i + (chunkIndex or 0)) * 17)) % STREAM_CHAIN_MOD
				end
				return NormalizeStreamState(guard + #blob + (hasPointer and 97 or 193))
			end

			local function AdvanceStreamState(chainState, blob, seed, chunkIndex, streamTag, hasPointer)
				local nextState = NormalizeStreamState((chainState or 0) + seed + ((streamTag or 0) * 73) + (hasPointer and 11 or 23) + ((chunkIndex or 0) * 29))
				for i = 1, #blob do
					nextState = (nextState * 131 + byte(blob, i) + (i * 7)) % STREAM_CHAIN_MOD
				end
				return NormalizeStreamState(nextState + #blob + 1)
			end

			local function DecodeStreamChunk(blob, seed, chainState, chunkIndex, streamTag)
				blob = DecodeCustom85(blob)
				local resolvedSeed = ResolveStreamSeed(seed, chainState, chunkIndex, streamTag)
				local output = {}
				for i = 1, #blob do
					local mask = (resolvedSeed + (i * 17)) % 251
					output[i] = char(bit32.bxor(byte(blob, i), mask))
				end
				return table.concat(output)
			end

			local function LoadStreamChunk(target, blob, seed, hasPointer, chainState, chunkIndex, streamTag, guard)
				local decoded = DecodeStreamChunk(blob, seed, chainState, chunkIndex, streamTag)
				local nextState = nil

				if chainState ~= nil then
					local expectedGuard = ComputeStreamGuard(decoded, chainState, seed, chunkIndex, streamTag, hasPointer)
					if expectedGuard ~= tonumber(guard) then
						error("corrupt vm stream")
					end
					nextState = AdvanceStreamState(chainState, decoded, seed, chunkIndex, streamTag, hasPointer)
				end

				local loadedMax = 0

				for segment in string.gmatch(decoded, "[^;]+") do
					if hasPointer then
						local pointerValue, family, slot = segment:match("^(%-?%d+)|(%-?%d+)|(%-?%d+)$")
						pointerValue = tonumber(pointerValue)
						family = tonumber(family)
						slot = tonumber(slot)

						if pointerValue then
							target[pointerValue] = { family, slot }
							if pointerValue > loadedMax then
								loadedMax = pointerValue
							end
						end
					else
						local family, slot = segment:match("^(%-?%d+)|(%-?%d+)$")
						family = tonumber(family)
						slot = tonumber(slot)

						if family then
							target[#target + 1] = { family, slot }
							loadedMax = #target
						end
					end
				end

				return loadedMax, nextState
			end

			local function lyq()
				local hooked = VQ3s["Iq0M1R"] == true
				local signal = tonumber(VQ3s["Hzwn"]) or 0
				return hooked, signal
			end

			local function STJFj(signal)
				local fake = {}
				local count = 0
				local mode = signal % 4
				local constantCount = #C

				if mode == 0 then
					count = 2
					fake[1] = false
					fake[2] = signal
				elseif mode == 1 then
					count = 1
					fake[1] = "JO0:" .. tostring(signal % 9973)
				elseif mode == 2 then
					count = 2
					fake[1] = signal % 2 == 0
					fake[2] = h3PDSU
				else
					count = 1
					if constantCount > 0 then
						fake[1] = C[(signal % constantCount) + 1]
					end
					if fake[1] == nil then
						fake[1] = signal
					end
				end

				return fake, count
			end

			local function S0KQM(f3bt, qZFW02, signal)

				if decoyCount == 0 then
					return
				end

				if not descriptor then
					return
				end

				local runner = f3bt.GKV[descriptor[1]]
				if runner then
					DecodeWindow = true
					runner(descriptor[2], qZFW02)
					DecodeWindow = false
				end
			end

	local isdW = "0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz!#$&()*+-:;<=>?@^_`{|}~"
	local PTGfC = {}
	for i = 1, #isdW do
		PTGfC[isdW:sub(i, i)] = i - 1
	end

	local function _uwU0b(input)
		local CVMO0 = {}
		local M2z = #input
		local z9 = 1

		while z9 <= M2z do
			local SIIXrW = math.min(5, M2z - z9 + 1)
			local fY7O2B = 0

			for Q7w = 0, 4 do
				local xe4N = input:sub(z9 + Q7w, z9 + Q7w)
				local VELG1 = PTGfC[xe4N]
				if VELG1 == nil then
					VELG1 = 84
				end
				if Q7w >= SIIXrW then
					VELG1 = 84
				end
				fY7O2B = fY7O2B * 85 + VELG1
			end

			local TTJ = {
				math.floor(fY7O2B / 16777216) % 256,
				math.floor(fY7O2B / 65536) % 256,
				math.floor(fY7O2B / 256) % 256,
				fY7O2B % 256
			}

			for z7 = 1, math.max(0, SIIXrW - 1) do
				CVMO0[#CVMO0 + 1] = string.char(TTJ[z7])
			end

			z9 = z9 + SIIXrW
		end

		return table.concat(CVMO0)
	end

	str = _uwU0b(str)
	local Hx7T = {}
	local EL6jT = #key
	local HoOydE = string.byte
	local gwQm8T = string.char
	local KAw3 = bit32 and bit32.KAw3 or function(a, b)
		local r, p = 0, 1
		for _ = 1, 8 do
			if a % 2 ~= b % 2 then r = r + p end
			a, b, p = (a - a % 2) / 2, (b - b % 2) / 2, p * 2
		end
		return r
	end
	for i = 1, #str do
		Hx7T[i] = gwQm8T(KAw3(HoOydE(str, i), HoOydE(key, (i - 1) % EL6jT + 1)))
	end
	return table.concat(Hx7T)
end
) end)()
